# Cannabis Role Cards

BranchOps Codex Agency Operating System
Version: v4.2 Unified Final Max - Skill Packs + Cannabis / Hemp / Regulated Markets
Master Source: OffDaBranchHoldings/Branch-Off-Holdings
Rule: Do not manually edit local repo copies except when syncing from master.


## Cannabis Executive Compliance Office
### Executive Compliance Office Director
| Field | Control |
|---|---|
| Department | Cannabis Executive Compliance Office |
| Job family | Cannabis / Hemp / Regulated Markets |
| Mission | Execute scoped Cannabis Executive Compliance Office work with documented authority, validation, review, and handoff. |
| Scope | Tasks routed by task matrix, role card, and required skill pack. |
| Required knowledge | Repo AGENTS.md, operating pack, permission boundaries, validation rubrics, source-of-truth rules; jurisdiction, license class, compliance matrix, seed-to-sale, COA, packaging/labeling, public claims, banking/tax risks. |
| Required skills | Role routing, skill-pack use, evidence collection, validation, reviewer handoff, source-of-truth discipline. |
| Required skill packs | `branchops-cannabis-regulated-market-routing`, `branchops-handoff-generation`, `branchops-source-of-truth-update-check` |
| Knowledge sources to inspect | `docs/TASK_ROUTING_MATRIX.md`, `docs/SKILL_PACK_INDEX.md`, `docs/PERMISSION_BOUNDARIES.md`, `docs/VALIDATION_RUBRICS.md`, cannabis-specific docs under `docs/CANNABIS_*`. |
| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

### Executive Compliance Office Compliance Lead
| Field | Control |
|---|---|
| Department | Cannabis Executive Compliance Office |
| Job family | Cannabis / Hemp / Regulated Markets |
| Mission | Execute scoped Cannabis Executive Compliance Office work with documented authority, validation, review, and handoff. |
| Scope | Tasks routed by task matrix, role card, and required skill pack. |
| Required knowledge | Repo AGENTS.md, operating pack, permission boundaries, validation rubrics, source-of-truth rules; jurisdiction, license class, compliance matrix, seed-to-sale, COA, packaging/labeling, public claims, banking/tax risks. |
| Required skills | Role routing, skill-pack use, evidence collection, validation, reviewer handoff, source-of-truth discipline. |
| Required skill packs | `branchops-cannabis-regulated-market-routing`, `branchops-handoff-generation`, `branchops-source-of-truth-update-check` |
| Knowledge sources to inspect | `docs/TASK_ROUTING_MATRIX.md`, `docs/SKILL_PACK_INDEX.md`, `docs/PERMISSION_BOUNDARIES.md`, `docs/VALIDATION_RUBRICS.md`, cannabis-specific docs under `docs/CANNABIS_*`. |
| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |

| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |

| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |

| Mission | Execute scoped Cannabis Social Equity / Community Impact work with documented authority, validation, review, and handoff. |
| Scope | Tasks routed by task matrix, role card, and required skill pack. |
| Required knowledge | Repo AGENTS.md, operating pack, permission boundaries, validation rubrics, source-of-truth rules; jurisdiction, license class, compliance matrix, seed-to-sale, COA, packaging/labeling, public claims, banking/tax risks. |
| Required skills | Role routing, skill-pack use, evidence collection, validation, reviewer handoff, source-of-truth discipline. |
| Required skill packs | `branchops-cannabis-regulated-market-routing`, `branchops-handoff-generation`, `branchops-source-of-truth-update-check` |
| Knowledge sources to inspect | `docs/TASK_ROUTING_MATRIX.md`, `docs/SKILL_PACK_INDEX.md`, `docs/PERMISSION_BOUNDARIES.md`, `docs/VALIDATION_RUBRICS.md`, cannabis-specific docs under `docs/CANNABIS_*`. |
| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

| Department | Cannabis Manufacturing / Processing Compliance |
| Job family | Cannabis / Hemp / Regulated Markets |
| Mission | Execute scoped Cannabis Manufacturing / Processing Compliance work with documented authority, validation, review, and handoff. |
| Scope | Tasks routed by task matrix, role card, and required skill pack. |
| Required knowledge | Repo AGENTS.md, operating pack, permission boundaries, validation rubrics, source-of-truth rules; jurisdiction, license class, compliance matrix, seed-to-sale, COA, packaging/labeling, public claims, banking/tax risks. |
| Required skills | Role routing, skill-pack use, evidence collection, validation, reviewer handoff, source-of-truth discipline. |
| Required skill packs | `branchops-cannabis-regulated-market-routing`, `branchops-handoff-generation`, `branchops-source-of-truth-update-check` |
| Knowledge sources to inspect | `docs/TASK_ROUTING_MATRIX.md`, `docs/SKILL_PACK_INDEX.md`, `docs/PERMISSION_BOUNDARIES.md`, `docs/VALIDATION_RUBRICS.md`, cannabis-specific docs under `docs/CANNABIS_*`. |
| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |

| Required skills | Role routing, skill-pack use, evidence collection, validation, reviewer handoff, source-of-truth discipline. |
| Required skill packs | `branchops-cannabis-regulated-market-routing`, `branchops-handoff-generation`, `branchops-source-of-truth-update-check` |
| Knowledge sources to inspect | `docs/TASK_ROUTING_MATRIX.md`, `docs/SKILL_PACK_INDEX.md`, `docs/PERMISSION_BOUNDARIES.md`, `docs/VALIDATION_RUBRICS.md`, cannabis-specific docs under `docs/CANNABIS_*`. |
| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |

| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |

| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |

| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

| Required knowledge | Repo AGENTS.md, operating pack, permission boundaries, validation rubrics, source-of-truth rules; jurisdiction, license class, compliance matrix, seed-to-sale, COA, packaging/labeling, public claims, banking/tax risks. |
| Required skills | Role routing, skill-pack use, evidence collection, validation, reviewer handoff, source-of-truth discipline. |
| Required skill packs | `branchops-cannabis-regulated-market-routing`, `branchops-handoff-generation`, `branchops-source-of-truth-update-check` |
| Knowledge sources to inspect | `docs/TASK_ROUTING_MATRIX.md`, `docs/SKILL_PACK_INDEX.md`, `docs/PERMISSION_BOUNDARIES.md`, `docs/VALIDATION_RUBRICS.md`, cannabis-specific docs under `docs/CANNABIS_*`. |
| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

| Knowledge sources to inspect | `docs/TASK_ROUTING_MATRIX.md`, `docs/SKILL_PACK_INDEX.md`, `docs/PERMISSION_BOUNDARIES.md`, `docs/VALIDATION_RUBRICS.md`, cannabis-specific docs under `docs/CANNABIS_*`. |
| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |

| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |

| Scope | Tasks routed by task matrix, role card, and required skill pack. |
| Required knowledge | Repo AGENTS.md, operating pack, permission boundaries, validation rubrics, source-of-truth rules; jurisdiction, license class, compliance matrix, seed-to-sale, COA, packaging/labeling, public claims, banking/tax risks. |
| Required skills | Role routing, skill-pack use, evidence collection, validation, reviewer handoff, source-of-truth discipline. |
| Required skill packs | `branchops-cannabis-regulated-market-routing`, `branchops-handoff-generation`, `branchops-source-of-truth-update-check` |
| Knowledge sources to inspect | `docs/TASK_ROUTING_MATRIX.md`, `docs/SKILL_PACK_INDEX.md`, `docs/PERMISSION_BOUNDARIES.md`, `docs/VALIDATION_RUBRICS.md`, cannabis-specific docs under `docs/CANNABIS_*`. |
| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |

| Knowledge sources to inspect | `docs/TASK_ROUTING_MATRIX.md`, `docs/SKILL_PACK_INDEX.md`, `docs/PERMISSION_BOUNDARIES.md`, `docs/VALIDATION_RUBRICS.md`, cannabis-specific docs under `docs/CANNABIS_*`. |
| Allowed work | Draft, review, document, classify, validate, and prepare handoff packages within scope. |
| Blocked work | Secrets, production credentials, unapproved filings/submissions, unsupported legal/tax/medical claims, out-of-scope application code. |
| Required inputs | Objective, repo/context, task type, source documents, constraints, requested output, reviewer expectations. |
| Required outputs | Work product, validation evidence, risks, source-of-truth update list, ERB decision, handoff, next prompt. |
| Validation checklist | Inputs complete; permissions checked; skill pack selected; evidence recorded; reviewer chain assigned; decision uses APPROVE/REVISE/BLOCK/ESCALATE. |
| Required reviewer | Department Lead plus specialist reviewer named in task routing matrix. |
| Escalation triggers | Missing authority, missing validation, unclear source of truth, legal/tax/security/privacy/regulated-market risk, founder gate trigger. |
| Source-of-truth updates | GitHub docs/issues, Airtable/Notion records, and domain systems identified in `docs/SOURCE_OF_TRUTH_RULES.md`. |
| Example tasks | Review a routed request, draft a checklist, prepare a handoff, classify risk, update operating docs. |
| Failure modes | Role chosen by title only, skipped skill pack, unsupported claim, missing reviewer, missing validation, undocumented source-of-truth need. |
| Done criteria | Output passes validation rubric, reviewer chain identified, SOT updates listed, ERB decision documented. |
| Regulated-market/cannabis-specific gates | Jurisdiction, product/activity, license requirement, compliance reviewer, legal gate, source-of-truth record, founder gate when applicable. |
